 On this day, infinite auspicious results can be obtained
 atah is din ko anant chaturdashi bhi kehete hai

 What is the method of immersion? - It is important to keep fast on this day
 - ghar main sthapit pratimaa kaa vidhiwatpujanakaren, pujan main nariyal, shami patr or doob jarur arpit karen

 - pratimaa ko le jate samay bhagwaan ganesh ko samarpit akshat ghar main avashya bikher den
 - Do not keep leather belt, watch and purse close, immerse yourself in bare feet
 - plastic keemurtior chitra na to sthapit karen or na hi visarjan karen, mitti kii pratimaa sarvshereshth he

 - bhojaptr yaa pile kaagaj par sabase upar swastik banaaen

 - Do not beat the handwriting and do not write anything behind the paper
 - samasyaon ke ant main apana naam likhen phir ganesh mantra likhen

 - samast samasyaon se mukti milegi
